                                                    Internet Printing Protocol (IPP) Registrations

   Created
           2002-07-15

   Last Updated
           2015-11-23

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           XML [IMG]
           HTML [IMG]
           Plain text

   Registries included below

     * Objects
     * Attributes
     * Keyword Attribute Values
     * Enum Attribute Values
     * Attribute Group Tags
     * Out-of-Band Attribute Value Tags
     * Attribute Syntaxes
     * Operations
     * Status Codes

Objects

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Mailing list and Expert Review

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Object definitions may be proposed as extensions to the base IPP protocol with
 an Expert Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to
 [RFC2911] section 6.2.  Objects are listed in alphabetic order.  The
 specifications that define objects, also define operations and attributes for
 the objects.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

       Name      Reference
   Document     [PWG5100.5]
   Job          [RFC2911]
   Printer      [RFC2911]
   Subscription [RFC3995]

Attributes

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Mailing list and Expert Review

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Attribute definitions may be proposed as extensions to the base IPP protocol
 with an Expert Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to
 [RFC2911] section 6.2. Attribute are listed in alphabetic order.  The member
 attributes of collection attributes [RFC3382] are indented two spaces
 immediately after the collection attribute to which they belong.

 The "xxx" Job Template attributes are Job object attributes, while the
 "xxx-default" and "xxx-supported" Job Template attributes are Printer object
 attributes.  See [RFC2911] Section 4.2 Job Template Attributes.

 The "xxx" Subscription Template attributes are Subscription object
 attributes, while the "xxx-default" and "xxx-supported" Subscription
 Template attributes are Printer object attributes.â€  See [RFC3995] Section
 5.2 Subscription Template Attributes.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

Attribute Group Tags

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Expert Review and mailing list/assignment

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Attribute Group Tags, Out-of-Band Attribute Value Tags, and Attribute Syntaxes share the same number space.

 The range of Attribute Group Tags is 0x00 to 0x0F.  Tag values are allocated
 using an Expert Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to
 [RFC2911] section 6.7.  See [RFC2910] section 3.5.2.  The tag values are
 listed in numeric order.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

     Value                  Name                  Reference
   0x00      Unassigned
   0x01      "operation-attributes-tag"          [RFC2910]
   0x02      "job-attributes-tag"                [RFC2910]
   0x03      "end-of-attributes-tag"             [RFC2910]
   0x04      "printer-attributes-tag"            [RFC2910]
   0x05      "unsupported-attributes-tag"        [RFC2910]
   0x06      "subscription-attributes-tag"       [RFC3995]
   0x07      "event-notification-attributes-tag" [RFC3995]
   0x08      Reserved (ipp-get-resources)
   0x09      document-attributes-tag             [PWG5100.5]
   0x0A-0x0F Unassigned

Out-of-Band Attribute Value Tags

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Expert Review and mailing list/assignment

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Attribute Group Tags, Out-of-Band Attribute Value Tags, and Attribute Syntaxes share the same number space.

 The range of out-of-band tags is 0x10 to 0x1F.  Tag values are allocated
 using an Expert Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to
 [RFC2911] section 6.7.  See [RFC2910] section 3.5.2.  The tag values are
 listed in numeric order.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

     Value             Name            Reference
   0x10      Unsupported               [RFC2910]
   0x11      Unassigned
   0x12      unknown                   [RFC2910]
   0x13      no-value                  [RFC2910]
   0x14      Reserved (ipp-col)
   0x15      not-settable              [RFC3380]
   0x16      delete-attribute          [RFC3380]
   0x17      admin-define              [RFC3380]
   0x18      Reserved (ipp-prod-print)
   0x19      Reserved (ipp-prod-print)
   0x1A-0x1F Unassigned

Attribute Syntaxes

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Expert Review and mailing list/assignment

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Attribute Group Tags, Out-of-Band Attribute Value Tags, and Attribute Syntaxes share the same number space.

 The range of attribute syntaxes is 0x20 to 0xFF.  Unassigned Tag values are allocated
 using an Expert Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to
 [RFC2911] section 6.3.  Use of the 0x7F value permits additional values up to
 0x3FFFFFFF for Expert Review action and 0x40000000 to 0x7FFFFFFF for vendor
 extensions.  See [RFC2910] section 3.5.2.  The tag values are listed in
 numeric order.

 0x20 is reserved for "generic integer" if it should ever be needed.

 0x40 is reserved for "generic character-string" if it should ever be
 needed.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

     Value                                                 Name                                                Reference
   0x20      Unassigned
   0x21      integer                                                                                           [RFC2910]
   0x22      boolean                                                                                           [RFC2910]
   0x23      enum                                                                                              [RFC2910]
   0x24-0x2F Unassigned - to be for integer data types                                                         [RFC2910]
   0x30      octetString with an unspecified format                                                            [RFC2910]
   0x31      dateTime                                                                                          [RFC2910]
   0x32      resolution                                                                                        [RFC2910]
   0x33      rangeOfInteger                                                                                    [RFC2910]
   0x34      begCollection                                                                                     [RFC3382]
   0x35      textWithLanguage                                                                                  [RFC2910]
   0x36      nameWithLanguage                                                                                  [RFC2910]
   0x37      endCollection                                                                                     [RFC3382]
   0x38-0x3F Unassigned - to be for octetString data types                                                     [RFC2910]
   0x40      Unassigned
   0x41      textWithoutLanguage                                                                               [RFC2910]
   0x42      nameWithoutLanguage                                                                               [RFC2910]
   0x43      Reserved for future IANA Registration after an Expert Review as defined in [RFC2911] section 6.3. [RFC2910]
   0x44      keyword                                                                                           [RFC2910]
   0x45      uri                                                                                               [RFC2910]
   0x46      uriScheme                                                                                         [RFC2910]
   0x47      charset                                                                                           [RFC2910]
   0x48      naturalLanguage                                                                                   [RFC2910]
   0x49      mimeMediaType                                                                                     [RFC2910]
   0x4A      memberAttrName                                                                                    [RFC3382]
   0x4B-0x5F Unassigned - to be for character-string data types                                                [RFC2910]
   0x60-0x7E Unassigned
   0x7F      For extension using the next 4 octets - see Note above.                                           [RFC2910]
   0x80-0xFF Unassigned

Operations

   Registration Procedure(s)

 RFC (standards track) and Expert Review/assignment

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 Operation definitions may be proposed as extensions to the base IPP protocol
 with a required review according to [RFC2911] section 6.4.  See the hex values
 assigned to each operation under the "operations-supported" attribute in
 Section 3 above.  In addition, vendors may define their own private operations.
 See the explanation at the beginning of Section 3 above on the enum allocation
 for such vendor-defined private operations.

 Operations are listed in alphabetic order.  Specifications that extend the
 semantics of operations defined in other specifications will be listed here
 as well on separate lines with the notation "(extension)" after the name.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

                    Name                       Reference
   Acknowledge-Document                    [PWG5100.18]
   Acknowledge-Identify-Printer            [PWG5100.18]
   Acknowledge-Job                         [PWG5100.18]
   Activate-Printer                        [RFC3998]
   Activate-Printer(deprecated)            [APPLE20150505-3]
   Add-Document-Images                     [PWG5100.15]
   Cancel-Current-Job                      [RFC3998]
   Cancel-Current-Job(extension)           [PWG5100.5]
   Cancel-Document                         [PWG5100.5]
   Cancel-Job                              [RFC2911]

Status Codes

   Registration Procedure(s)

 Expert Review and mailing list/assignment

   Expert(s)

 Ira McDonald, Michael Sweet

   Reference
           [RFC2911]

   Note

 The range of status code values is 0x0000 to 0x7FFF.  Status code values are allocated using an Expert
 Review that requires a review with a mailing list according to [RFC2911]
 section 6.6.  [RFC2911] section 13 allocates the value ranges for each status
 code class as follows:

   "successful"     - 0x0000 to 0x00FF
   "informational"  - 0x0100 to 0x01FF
   Unassigned       - 0x0200 to 0x02FF
   "redirection"    - 0x0300 to 0x03FF   -- See [RFC2911] Errata
   "client-error"   - 0x0400 to 0x04FF
   "server-error"   - 0x0500 to 0x05FF
   Unassigned       - 0x0600 to 0x7FFF

 Values in the range 0x0080 to 0x05FF are reserved for vendor extensions.
 The top half (128 values) of each range (0x0n80 See [RFC2911] Errata) to
 0x0nFF, for n = 0 to 5) is reserved for vendor use within each status code
 class.  Status codes are
 listed in numeric order.

   Available Formats
           [IMG]
           CSV

       Value                           Name                         Reference
   0x0000        successful-ok                                     [RFC2911]
   0x0001        successful-ok-ignored-or-substituted-attributes   [RFC2911]
   0x0002        successful-ok-conflicting-attributes              [RFC2911]
   0x0003        successful-ok-ignored-subscriptions               [RFC3995]
   0x0004        Reserved (ipp-indp-method)

   0x0006        Reserved (ipp-indp-method)
